\DoxyCodeLine{06510\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06511\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ If\ a\ subjectAltName\ extension\ of\ type\ dNSName\ is\ present,\ that\ MUST}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06513\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ field\ in\ the\ Subject\ field\ of\ the\ certificate\ MUST\ be\ used.\ Although}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06514\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ the\ use\ of\ the\ Common\ Name\ is\ existing\ practice,\ it\ is\ deprecated\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06515\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Certification\ Authorities\ are\ encouraged\ to\ use\ the\ dNSName\ instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06516\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06517\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Matching\ is\ performed\ using\ the\ matching\ rules\ specified\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06518\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ [RFC2459].\ \ If\ more\ than\ one\ identity\ of\ a\ given\ type\ is\ present\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06519\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ the\ certificate\ (e.g.,\ more\ than\ one\ dNSName\ name,\ a\ match\ in\ any\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06520\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ of\ the\ set\ is\ considered\ acceptable.)\ Names\ may\ contain\ the\ wildcard}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06521\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ character\ *\ which\ is\ considered\ to\ match\ any\ single\ domain\ name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06522\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ component\ or\ component\ fragment.\ E.g.,\ *.a.com\ matches\ foo.a.com\ but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06523\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ not\ bar.foo.a.com.\ f*.com\ matches\ foo.com\ but\ not\ bar.com.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06524\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06526\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ hostname.\ In\ this\ case,\ the\ iPAddress\ subjectAltName\ must\ be\ present}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06527\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ in\ the\ certificate\ and\ must\ exactly\ match\ the\ IP\ in\ the\ URI.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06528\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
